< text>
Prices seemed low... until we got our food. Then they made sense. We ordered a 6"pastrami sandwich, 6" chicken parmesan sandwich, an order of chicken strips & 2 fountain drinks. The pastrami was flavorful, just a very thin sandwich. The chicken parm sandwich was very obviously a single chicken strip with mediocre sauce and a generous portion of mozzarella. The chicken strips. They were very clearly premade frozen strips available in any grocery store. They were baked, rather than fried. Carl's Jr. has significantly better chicken strips, for a comparable price. Both the fountain drinks [orange soda & raspberry tea] tasted as though they had been partially filled, then topped off with plain water. It was very clear why we were the only customers during the lunch rush [just after 12pm].</text>

< Text>
In short, this clinic is a typical profit-centered, incompetent business rather than a proper veterinary clinic that offers service to care for animals' lives and get paid for it. I would never trust them again. For those who are interested, below is my latest experience with them in detail:

We had to get an international health certificate for our cat. Few months prior to our departure, I was in contact with the clinic about the health certificate requirements. The person who was working there was particularly very helpful. Those who have travelled with their pets would know how incredibly bureaucratic, complicated and costly is the process of getting together of an animal's travel documents. That's why I have talked to USDA and this clinic several times prior to our departure.

5 days prior to our departure, we took our cat there to get the last examination, necessary treatments and the international health certificate. During the examination, I had to remind Dr. Sellers various requirements (treatment against ticks and tapeworms) that she was not aware of. Initially, she had filled and printed an outdated version of international health certificate required by Turkey (can be very easily avoided if you just google it). They had changed it after my warning. My impression was that Dr. Sellers was being reckless about something that she was not very experienced. I do not expect her to fully know each country's requirements. Precisely for this reason, she should have been much more careful. But, she clearly had not done her homework about something this serious and important. Nevertheless, I had still had my trust to the documents she had signed as she must have done this several times and knew at least where (not) to sign. As required, I went to USDA office in Los Angeles on the date of my travel. I had found out that, Dr. Sellers had completely messed up with the document. She had not only missed her signature and date&time information in required spaces but also wrongly signed another space (so her reply to my partner's review is not accurate). The document was useless. We had exactly 1 hour and 20 minutes to get a new health certificate in LA. We got lucky and found a nearby vet to which we had to pay $253 ($186 for health certificate and $67 for examination). I managed to get the approval from the USDA literally at the last minute. When I called this clinic, they admitted the mistake only after a while and told me that they can refund me the price of the health certificate which was 25$. Later, they said they can refund the price of examination too ($50). However, the least they could do was to refund me the total cost of the second vet clinic in addition. Of course, the emotional stress that we had to go through cannot be reimbursed at all.

This could be a whole different scenario if I had my appointment with USDA 15 minutes later or could not bring together $250. That is why the mistake Dr. Sellers has done and the way this clinic has handled it afterwards is not only problematic from a business point of view but grossly unethical as a veterinarian! As she was not meticulous as she needed to be from the beginning, this is not simply an honest mistake either. My request to speak to Dr. Sellers was denied when I asked for. She did not even care to apologize to me personally. Rather they told me that they have found my partner's google review very rude and hung up on me.

Clearly, they prioritize the reputation of their business over the well being of the animals that they supposedly care for and get paid in return.</Text>

< text>
I came home after work one night and found my 8-yo cat unable to pee.  I took him to a different emergency clinic and they unblocked and relieved him, but went on to explain that he had bladder stones, kidney failure, and would likely block again without performing a surgery to remove the stones.  I didnt have insurance and was $3k into this for the overnight visit, before the surgery! They provided a great service but were 3-4 times the cost of the cat and bird clinic, so I had cat and bird perform the surgery.  Dr Pruett and Dr Sellars did an excellent job, made me feel comfortable and took great care of my boy.  Despite the surgery, he blocked again immediately, but not from a stone this time.  He ended up staying overnight for an extended period of time while we tried to find the cause of the blockage.  During this time, I made daily visits and got to see the behind the scenes care that goes into all the animals they treat.  Cat and bird clinic has an excellent team and every animal there gets love an attention.  My story unfortunately doesnt have a positive outcome but I can walk away feeling confident that I took my cat to the right place.

Lessons to pass on:
*Dont feed your cats dry food, especially the male cats.
*Get pet insurance, its cheap, will save you thousands.
*Learn what signs to look for that indicate your pet has a health issue and address early on.</text>

< Review>
I waited two hours to be seen, but that's to be expected for urgent care. The PA that saw me was reasonably attentive and responded to my needs. They did x-rays of my arm on site.  All was well up to that point.  They concluded I likely had  mild fracture in my elbow. An LVN then prepared a splint to immobilize it.  I later realized the splint goes too far down my hand, and was therefore more inconvenient than it needed to be.  Still, I was glad to not have to endure an ER visit.  They set a follow-up appt one week out.

The bill ended up to be significantly more than I expected and I was not allowed to have a breakdown of the bill unless I agreed to waive the cash-pay discount that they offer.  I learned a week later, after following up with an orthopedic surgeon elsewhere, that I did not have a fracture, which was a relief.  Treating it like a fracture by splinting it was not a bad thing for my injury, however, but it ended up costing me a lot more due to the diagnosis.

Bottom line:  The medical treatment is not bad, but if you think you might have a mild fracture, it may be best to go to the ER or to an orthopedist first.  It's doubtful you will save any money by going to the urgent care.  If you decide to go to the clinic and are a cash-pay patient, know that their discount comes at the price of not seeing the itemization of the charges.

I did have a nice phone conversation with their practice administrator after I initially posted, which was very pleasant. She said they are looking into ways to handle the cash-pay/itemization waiver issue.  It sounds like they sincerely want to be a good and transparent provider for the community.<//Review>

<gmapID>0x80dd3169a18b0cdb:0xae9a9729ce2c9abf</gmapID>< Review>
The very best PHO on Anaheim, possibly even all of long beach. This place it's very cozy, the service was fast and responsive to our needs. I don't eat out at Asian food places much but today i was in real need of some delicious hot soup soul food. My first and definitely not my last time coming here. I ordered the beef with tendon, it was hearty and delicious. The tendon was very soft and the broth needed very little extra seasoning. For the price of the regular pho bowl it was enough to get me full, and I like to eat a lot when i get the munchies! Definitely worth the visit.</Review>

<rating>5< /rating>< review>
I'm so relieved that they are open during the pandemic! This pho place has always been my favorite pho in LA county. I have tried so many other places but nothing compares to this place. Everything from the customer service, to the tidiness, to the food is simply exquisite! I've been a recurring customer for roughly ten years and I have never been disappointed! To begin with, when we entered they warmly greeted us with a big smile. Also, the restaurant is always clean. The food is really good for such a cheap price. They are generous with their portions and meals. I used to order: chicken breast (ga Uc: g1) or (ga dui: g2). Sometimes, I either took rare steak (pho tai p2) or well-done flank (pho tai Chin P4). My family loves their spring rolls and combo fried rice. For the drinks. we took Thai tea and Iced coffee. i also appreciate their honesty. Over the years my family, my friends and I have the bad habits to forget many valuable items when we left the restaurant such as : Iphone, credit card, laptop, purses belonging to an expensive brand... They ran after us in order to return our missing belongings. We would've lost a good amount of valuable items if it weren't for their help! This place has a big parking, so check them out and you won't regret it! Additionally, they are doing dine-ins once again but with social distancing.<//review>

< Review>
New Pho has great Pho and a fantastic staff!
I am picky about my Pho so trust me when I say this place is great!
The broth is delicious and not watered down. They are super generous here with the meat, noodles and veggies (my favorite) so generous that if I had one complaint it would be that I would like more broth!
Prices are super affordable and fair. They accept credit cards and have a nice sized parking lot on the side where the entrance is actually located also another good thing about this spot is they do delivery through PostMates!
Definitely will be back again and recommend anyone in the area to try it if they are looking for genuine Pho.</Review>

<Review>Such an awesome experience. I spent my 30th birthday here. Initially I was going to have a private party but ended up canceling it so I did a bottomless brunch paint day instead. Setting up the private party and canceling it was very easy to do. The bottles brunch was $45 and worth every penny. You got two sizeable pieces of chicken and a big ole waffle and bottomless mimosas. They are not skimpy or stingy with the mimosas. Most people had between two and three because honestly, you came to paint not get drunk. The instruction is easy to follow, there's tons of laughter and it's a super safe space to be a black woman, though all are welcome. I will come back again and again. I'm in love with my painting and am still shocked by how great it turned out. I can't recommend it enough.<//Review><Name>Krystal withak< /Name>< gmapID>
